# Cherry-pick revert of Inductor ReLU/GELU(Addmm) fusions (#168157)

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/pytorch--ca246612 (mirror of pytorch)
**Difficulty:** HARD
**Category:** cross_module_bug_fix



## Description

This is a cherry-pick of the revert of PR #168157, which added `Activation(Addmm) -> _addmm_activation` pattern replacement in the Inductor lowering pass.

PR #168157 introduced pattern matching in the Inductor compiler to fuse activation functions (ReLU, GELU) with Addmm (matrix multiply + bias add) operations into a single `_addmm_activation` call that leverages cuBLASLt's fused epilogue support. This optimization aimed to reduce kernel launches and memory traffic for common `Linear -> Activation` patterns.

However, the fusion caused regressions in certain model configurations and needed to be reverted. This cherry-pick applies the revert to the release branch, undoing:
- The `_addmm_activation` pattern replacement in Inductor's lowering/decomposition passes
- The associated pattern matcher registrations for ReLU(Addmm) and GELU(Addmm)
- Any cuBLASLt epilogue fusion paths added for these patterns

Changes:
- 4 files modified
- 93 additions, 87 deletions

## Task

Implement the fix: Cherry-pick revert of Inductor ReLU/GELU(Addmm) fusions

Description: Revert PR #168157 which added `Activation(Addmm) -> _addmm_activation` pattern replacement in the Inductor lowering pass for cuBLASLt fused epilogue support. The fusion caused regressions and needs to be reverted.

class TestPatternMatcherLogging(LoggingTestCase):
    device_type = GPU_TYPE

    @make_logging_test()
    def test_pattern_match_debug_output(self, records):
        def pattern(x, y):
            return x + y

        def replacement(x, y):
            return x * y

        my_patterns = PatternMatcherPass()
        inputs = [
            torch.randn(4, 4, device=GPU_TYPE),
            torch.randn(4, 4, device=GPU_TYPE),
        ]
        register_replacement(pattern, replacement, inputs, fwd_only, my_patterns)

        def custom_pass(graph: torch.fx.Graph):
            return my_patterns.apply(graph)

        def fn(x, y):
            return x + y

        x = torch.randn(4, 4, device=GPU_TYPE)
        y = torch.randn(4, 4, device=GPU_TYPE)

        with unittest.mock.patch.dict(
            os.environ, {"TORCHINDUCTOR_PATTERN_MATCH_DEBUG": "add"}
        ):
            compiled_fn = torch.compile(
                fn, options={"post_grad_custom_post_pass": custom_pass}
            )
            result = compiled_fn(x, y)
            self.assertEqual(result, x * y)

        specific_record = self.getRecord(records, "Specific pattern match")
        self.assertIn(
            "Match(..., [], {'x': arg0_1, 'y': arg1_1})", specific_record.getMessage()
        )
        self.assertIn("add(arg0_1, arg1_1)", specific_record.getMessage())

        def pattern(x):
            return x + 1

for i, line in enumerate(lines):
    if '@functools.cache' in line and i+1 < len(lines) and 'def register_addmm_activation_fusions' in lines[i+1]:
        func_start = i  # 0-indexed

assert func_start is not None, "Could not find function start"

func_end = None
for i in range(func_start+1, len(lines)):
    if '@init_once_fakemode' in lines[i]:
        func_end = i  # 0-indexed (first line after function's blank lines)

assert func_end is not None, "Could not find function end"

# But we need to keep TWO blank lines before @init_once_fakemode
# Check how many blank lines are between the function end and @init_once_fakemode
blank_count = 0
for i in range(func_end-1, func_start, -1):
    if lines[i].strip() == '':
        blank_count += 1
    else:
        break

print(f"Blank lines before @init_once_fakemode: {blank_count}")
print(f"Function at lines {func_start+1}-{func_end+1} (1-indexed)")
print(f"Deleting lines {func_start+1} to {func_end+1-blank_count} (1-indexed)")

# Actually from the diff: in pre-PR there were 2 blank lines before @init_once_fakemode
# The PR added function + 2 blank lines (lines 692-751 in first_merge)
# The revert deleted those exact lines, leaving the original 2 blank lines

# keeping just enough blank lines to match the pre-PR state (2 blank lines before @init_once_fakemode)

# In HEAD, before @init_once_fakemode there should be 2 blank lines total
# The function itself has blank_count blank lines at end
# We want to keep 2 blank lines, so delete the function MINUS (2 - blank_count_before_function) blanks
# Actually simpler: delete from func_start to func_end-2 (keep 2 blank lines before @init_once_fakemode)

blanks_before_func = 0
for i in range(func_start-1, -1, -1):
    if lines[i].strip() == '':
        blanks_before_func += 1
    else:
        break
print(f"Blank lines before @functools.cache: {blanks_before_func}")

# The function block to delete:
# We delete from func_start (the @functools.cache line) through the blank lines,
# but we need to keep at least 2 blank lines before @init_once_fakemode
# From the original revert: it deleted from @functools.cache through ONE of the two blanks

# Wait - but we saw the PRE-PR has 2 blank lines already

print(f"\nWill delete: lines {func_start+1} to {func_end} (0-indexed: {func_start} to {func_end-1})")
print(f"These are: {lines[func_start]!r} through {lines[func_end-1]!r}")

# Apply cherry-pick revert changes to post_grad.py

with open('/workspace/torch/_inductor/fx_passes/post_grad.py', 'r') as f:
    lines = f.readlines()

original_len = len(lines)

# 1. Remove gen_register_replacement import (line 37, 0-indexed 36)
assert '    gen_register_replacement,' in lines[36]
new_lines = lines[:36] + lines[37:]
lines = new_lines
print(f"After removing import: {len(lines)} lines (was {original_len})")

# 2. Remove register_addmm_activation_fusions function
# After removing the import, line numbers shift by -1
# Function was at 0-indexed 684 (1-indexed 685), now at 0-indexed 683 (after -1 shift)
func_start = None
for i, line in enumerate(lines):
    if '@functools.cache' in line and i+1 < len(lines) and 'def register_addmm_activation_fusions' in lines[i+1]:
        func_start = i
        break
assert func_start is not None, "Function not found"

# Find @init_once_fakemode to know where function ends
func_end = None
for i in range(func_start+1, len(lines)):
    if '@init_once_fakemode' in lines[i]:
        func_end = i
        break
assert func_end is not None

print(f"Function: 0-indexed {func_start}-{func_end-1}, deleting {func_end-func_start} lines")
new_lines = lines[:func_start] + lines[func_end:]
lines = new_lines
print(f"After removing function: {len(lines)} lines")

# 3. Remove register_addmm_activation_fusions() call and preceding blank line
call_line = None
for i, line in enumerate(lines):
    if '    register_addmm_activation_fusions()' in line:
        call_line = i
        break
assert call_line is not None

# Check blank line before
assert lines[call_line-1].strip() == '', f"Expected blank line before call, got: {lines[call_line-1]!r}"
print(f"Call at 0-indexed {call_line}, blank at {call_line-1}")

# Delete blank line and call
new_lines = lines[:call_line-1] + lines[call_line+1:]
lines = new_lines
print(f"After removing call+blank: {len(lines)} lines")

with open('/workspace/torch/_inductor/fx_passes/post_grad.py', 'w') as f:
    f.writelines(lines)

print(f"Done! Final file has {len(lines)} lines")

        break
assert test_end is not None, "Could not find end of test"
print(f"test_addmm_activation_fusion ends before 0-indexed {test_end} (1-indexed {test_end+1})")
print(f"Deleting {test_end - test_start} lines")

# Check what the next test is
print(f"Next test: {lines[test_end].rstrip()!r}")

new_lines = lines[:test_start] + lines[test_end:]
lines = new_lines
print(f"After removing test: {len(lines)} lines")

# 2. Find and fix test_addmm_alpha_beta_with_pointwise
# Change torch.abs to torch.nn.functional.relu
changes = 0
for i, line in enumerate(lines):
    if 'torch.abs(torch.addmm(' in line:
        new_line = line.replace('torch.abs(torch.addmm(', 'torch.nn.functional.relu(torch.addmm(')
        lines[i] = new_line
        print(f"Fixed line {i+1}: {new_line.rstrip()!r}")
        changes += 1

print(f"Fixed {changes} torch.abs → torch.nn.functional.relu changes")

with open('/workspace/test/inductor/test_pattern_matcher.py', 'w') as f:
    f.writelines(lines)

print(f"Done! Final file has {len(lines)} lines")
